    <script type="text/javascript">
		var myPop;
		var myForm;

		function showPlotNotes(inp) {
			if (!myPop) {
				myPop = new dhtmlXPopup();
				myPop.attachHTML("Some complex Browse query constraints may be ignored in Xamin.");
			}
			if (myPop.isVisible()) {
				myPop.hide();
			} else {
				var x = window.dhx4.absLeft(inp);
				var y = window.dhx4.absTop(inp);
				var w = inp.offsetWidth;
				var h = inp.offsetHeight;
				myPop.show(x,y,w,h);
			}
		}

		function hidePopup() {
			if (myPop) myPop.hide();
		}
    </script>

//function checks if user has entered input where necessary
function pageCheck() {
        //check if the browser is valid
        var nav = navigator.appName;
        var ver = navigator.appVersion;

        if (nav == "") { return(true); }
        if (nav == "Microsoft Internet Explorer") {
          if ((ver.charAt(0)) < 2) { return(true); }
        }

        // initialize input values as invalid
        var target_check  = false;
        var retrieveset_check  = false;

        //initialize input as invalid and get entered values from form
        //var target_check = false;
        var target_check;
        var flds = document.w3hdprods.elements;
        //has the checkbox been marked?
        for (var i=0; i<flds.length; i++) {
           var fld = flds[i];
           // does field name start with Target and is it checked?
           if ((fld.name.indexOf("Target")==0) && fld.checked) {
             target_check = true;
             break;

        }

        //initialize input as invalid and get entered values from form

  } // pageCheck()

function setcheckDP (val) {
  var checkdp=val;
}

  function tickTable(flds,ischecked,table) {
    if (flds) {
      if (flds.nodeName === 'INPUT') {
        flds.checked=ischecked;
      } else if (flds.length) {
        for (var i=0; i < flds.length; i++) {
          if ((table == '') || (flds[i].value.indexOf(table) > -1)) {
            flds[i].checked=ischecked;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return;
  }
  function tickTablestrict(flds,ischecked,string) {
    if (flds) {
      if (flds.nodeName === 'INPUT') {
        flds.checked=ischecked;
      } else if (flds.length) {
        for (var i=0; i < flds.length; i++) {
          if (flds[i].value == string) {
            flds[i].checked=ischecked;
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return;
  } //tickTablestrict() -->

<div style='visibility:hidden;' id='help' t_title='Help' title='Click to view Tabbed Display help'><!-- help -->
<p>General Browse help can be found at the <a href='/W3Browse/w3browse-help.html'>Browse Help</a> page.
<h3>Browse Tabbed Display</h3>
<textarea cols='80' rows='30' readonly style='border:0px #fff;'>
The tabbed Browse output organizes mission and table results in a set
of hierarchical tabbed panels.  Rather than having to navigate a vast
single page of results, users can jump from table to table.

The Query Information tab displays the criteria on which the search is
based, other display format options (i.e., HTML, Text), and the summary
of results table which lists all table names that match the criteria
and the number of rows in each table.  The table name is a link to the
tab displaying the table results.

The Query Results tab lists a tab for each mission (middle tab level) and a
tab for each table associated with each mission (bottom tab level).   To
display table results first select the mission tab and then the table tab.
The table tab will display all table results.  From there you can perform
table-related functions such as plotting and  cross-correlating as well as
selecting data products.  For data products select the table rows you are
interested in and the data products types.  These selected rows will now
appear under the Data Products Retrieval tab.

The Data Products Retrieval tab will display all data products that you have
selected.  From this page you can chose the download method to retrieve
the data products or choose Web-based Services options (e.g., SkyView images,
NED queries).  Deselect any data products you are no longer interested in
before downloading.
</textarea>
</div>
